mb-14" data-page-title="Manage Positions" data-page-href="/trading/positions/manage" id="content"><span data-as="p">Manage positions outside the order book by splitting collateral into complete
sets of outcome tokens, merging balanced tokens back into collateral, or
redeeming winning tokens after resolution.</span>
<span data-as="p">Choose an operation based on how you want to change your position:</span>
<!-- --><div role="presentation" style="position:relative;--scroll-area-corner-height:0px;--scroll-area-corner-width:0px" data-component-part="scroll-area" data-table-wrapper="true" class="min-w-0 [--page-padding:20px] flex w-[calc(100%+(var(--page-padding)*2))] my-[1em] py-[1em] -mx-(--page-padding) max-w-none [contain:inline-size]"><div role="region" data-id="base-ui-_R_2lcrrav5tccsmisnpfiulb_-viewport" tabindex="-1" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] overflow-y-hidden! base-ui-disable-scrollbar" style="overflow:scroll" data-component-part="scroll-area-viewport" aria-label="Scrollable table"><div role="presentation" style="min-width:fit-content" data-component-part="scroll-area-content" class="flex"><div class="px-(--page-padding) grow max-w-none table"><table class="m-0 min-w-full w-full max-w-none table [&amp;_td]:min-w-[150px] [&amp;_th]:text-left [&amp;_td[data-numeric]]:tabular-nums"><thead><tr><th>Operation</th><th>Use it when</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Split</td><td>You need to convert collateral into a complete set of outcome tokens.</td></tr><tr><td>Merge</td><td>You hold balanced outcome tokens and want to convert them back to collateral.</td></tr><tr><td>Redeem</td><td>A market has resolved and you want to claim collateral for winning positions.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div></div></div>
<span data-as="p">Choose the integration surface you will use to submit position operations.</span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">const</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> client</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> =</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0"> await</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> createSecureClient</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">({</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    ),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div></div></div><span data-as="p">The synchronous <code>SecureClient</code> provides the same methods and supports both
API key types.</span><span data-as="p">See <a class="link" href="/trading/wallets-auth#execute-gasless-transactions">Wallets and
Authentication</a> for the
complete wallet setup and Relayer authorization flow.</span></div><div id="panel-api-2" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="api" tabindex="0" class="prose dark:prose-invert overflow-x-auto [&amp;_[data-table-wrapper]]:![--page-padding:0px] [&amp;_[role=&quot;listitem&quot;]]:pl-4 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)_img]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child[data-table-wrapper]]:pt-0! hidden" data-component-part="tab-content"><span data-as="p">The examples on this page assume you can authenticate Relayer API requests

<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="split-a-position"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#split-a-position" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="size-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-xs text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" class="size-3 shrink-0"><path d="M8.50001 6.827C8.14801 6.995 7.81801 7.225 7.52701 7.517L7.51701 7.527C6.13601 8.908 6.13601 11.146 7.51701 12.527L9.69201 14.702C11.073 16.083 13.311 16.083 14.692 14.702L14.702 14.692C16.083 13.311 16.083 11.073 14.702 9.692L13.771 8.761" stroke="currentColor" width="1.5" linecap="round" linejoin="round"></path><path d="M9.50002 11.173C9.85202 11.005 10.182 10.775 10.473 10.483L10.483 10.473C11.864 9.092 11.864 6.854 10.483 5.473L8.30802 3.298C6.92702 1.917 4.68902 1.917 3.30802 3.298L3.29802 3.308C1.91702 4.689 1.91702 6.927 3.29802 8.308L4.22902 9.239" stroke="currentColor" width="1.5" linecap="round" linejoin="round"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Split a Position</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Splitting converts pUSD into a complete set of outcome tokens. Every 1 pUSD
produces 1 YES token and 1 NO token.</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 dark:twoslash-dark bg-transparent dark:bg-transparent" numberOfLines="2" language="text"><div data-floating-buttons="true" class="absolute top-3 right-4 flex items-center gap-1.5 print:hidden"><div aria-label="Copy the contents from the code block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" class="size-4 shrink-0 text-gray-400 group-hover/copy-button:text-gray-500 dark:text-white/40 dark:group-hover/copy-button:text-white/60"><path d="M14.25 5.25H7.25C6.14543 5.25 5.25 6.14543 5.25 7.25V14.25C5.25 15.3546 6.14543 16.25 7.25 16.25H14.25C15.3546 16.25 16.25 15.3546 16.25 14.25V7.25C16.25 6.14543 15.3546 5.25 14.25 5.25Z" stroke="currentColor" width="1.5" linecap="round" linejoin="round"></path><path d="M2.80103 11.998L1.77203 5.07397C1.61003 3.98097 2.36403 2.96397 class="sr-only"></span></div></div><div role="presentation" style="position:relative;--scroll-area-corner-height:0px;--scroll-area-corner-width:0px;font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E" class="line"><span>100 pUSD → 100 YES tokens + 100 NO tokens</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">Before splitting, ensure you have:</span>
<ol>
<li>Enough pUSD in the wallet for the amount you want to split.</li>
<li>Approved the collateral adapter for the market type to spend the wallet’s
pUSD.</li>
</ol>

<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">const</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> outcome</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> =</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0"> await</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> transaction</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">.</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">wait</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">();</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">// outcome.transactionHash: TxHash</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">// outcome.transactionId: TransactionId | null</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div><span data-as="p"><code>amount</code> is denominated in pUSD base units, so <code>1_000_000n</code> splits 1 pUSD
into 1 YES token and 1 NO token. <code>wait()</code> returns a <code>TransactionOutcome</code>
after the transaction settles.</span></div><div id="panel-python-2-1" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="python-2" tabindex="0" class="prose dark:prose-invert overflow-x-auto [&amp;_[data-table-wrapper]]:![--page-padding:0px] [&amp;_[role=&quot;listitem&quot;]]:pl-4 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)_img]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child[data-table-wrapper]]:pt-0! hidden" data-component-part="tab-content"><span data-as="p">Call <code>split_position()</code> on an <code>AsyncSecureClient</code>. type from the condition ID and select the correct collateral adapter.</span><div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 <span class="line"><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">  -H</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> &quot;RELAYER_API_KEY: </span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">$RELAYER_API_KEY</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">&quot;</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D7BA7D"> \</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">  -H</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> &quot;RELAYER_API_KEY_ADDRESS: </span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">$RELAYER_API_KEY_ADDRESS</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">&quot;</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D7BA7D"> \</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">  --data</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> &#x27;{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;WALLET&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    &quot;from&quot;: &quot;&lt;signer_address&gt;&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    &quot;to&quot;: &quot;0x00000000000Fb5C9ADea0298D729A0CB3823Cc07&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    &quot;nonce&quot;: &quot;&lt;wallet_nonce&gt;&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    &quot;signature&quot;: &quot;&lt;wallet_batch_signature&gt;&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    &quot;metadata&quot;: &quot;Split position&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    &quot;depositWalletParams&quot;: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">      &quot;depositWallet&quot;: &quot;&lt;deposit_wallet_address&gt;&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">      &quot;deadline&quot;: &quot;&lt;unix_seconds&gt;&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">      &quot;calls&quot;: [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">          &quot;target&quot;: &quot;&lt;collateral_adapter_address&gt;&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">          &quot;value&quot;: &quot;0&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">          &quot;data&quot;: &quot;&lt;encoded_split_position_calldata&gt;&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">      ]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">  }&#x27;</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div><span data-as="p">See <a class="link" href="/trading/wallets-auth#execute-gasless-transactions">Execute Gasless
Transactions</a> for nonce
creation, wallet-batch signing, and confirmation. Wait for
<code>STATE_CONFIRMED</code> before using the new balances.</span></div></div></div></div></div><div id="panel-solidity-2-3" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="solidity-2" tabindex="0" class="prose dark:prose-invert overflow-x-auto [&amp;_[data-table-wrapper]]:![--page-padding:0px] [&amp;_[role=&quot;listitem&quot;]]:pl-4 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)_img]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child[data-table-wrapper]]:pt-0! hidden" data-component-part="tab-content"><span data-as="p">Splitting pUSD through a collateral adapter follows this flow:</span><ul>
<li>Approve the collateral adapter to spend the amount of pUSD being split.</li>
<li>Call the adapter with the market’s condition ID and the amount.</li>
<li>The adapter executes the underlying CTF operation and mints equal YES and NO
balances atomically.</li>
</ul><div role="list" class="steps ml-3.5 mt-10 mb-6"><div role="listitem" class="step group/step step-container relative flex items-start pb-5"><div data-component-part="step-line" class="absolute w-px h-[calc(100%-2.75rem)] top-11 bg-gray-200/70 dark:bg-white/10" contentEditable="false"></div><div class="absolute ml-[-13px] py-2" data-component-part="step-number" contentEditable="false"><div class="group/step-indicator relative size-7 shrink-0 rounded-full bg-gray-50 dark:bg-white/10 text-xs text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-50 font-semibold flex items-center justify-center"><div class="group-has-[a:focus-visible]/step-indicator:opacity-0">1</div></div></div><div class="w-full overflow-hidden pl-8 pr-px"><p class="mt-2 font-semibold prose dark:prose-invert text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200" contentEditable="false" data-component-part="step-title">Approve pUSD</p><div data-component-part="step-content" class="prose dark:prose-invert"><span data-as="p">First, call <code>approve()</code> on the pUSD contract. Approve
<code>CtfCollateralAdapter</code> for a standard market or
<code>NegRiskCtfCollateralAdapter</code> for a negative-risk market:</span><div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 <h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="merge-positions"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#merge-positions" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="size-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-xs text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" class="size-3 shrink-0"><path d="M8.50001 6.827C8.14801 6.995 7.81801 7.225 7.52701 7.517L7.51701 7.527C6.13601 8.908 6.13601 11.146 7.51701 12.527L9.69201 14.702C11.073 16.083 13.311 16.083 14.692 14.702L14.702 14.692C16.083 13.311 16.083 11.073 14.702 9.692L13.771 8.761" stroke="currentColor" width="1.5" linecap="round" linejoin="round"></path><path d="M9.50002 11.173C9.85202 11.005 10.182 10.775 10.473 10.483L10.483 10.473C11.864 9.092 11.864 6.854 10.483 5.473L8.30802 3.298C6.92702 1.917 4.68902 1.917 3.30802 3.298L3.29802 3.308C1.91702 4.689 1.91702 6.927 3.29802 8.308L4.22902 9.239" stroke="currentColor" width="1.5" linecap="round" linejoin="round"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Merge Positions</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Merging converts a complete set of outcome tokens back into pUSD. Every 1 YES
token and 1 NO token returns 1 pUSD.</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 dark:twoslash-dark bg-transparent dark:bg-transparent" numberOfLines="2" language="text"><div data-floating-buttons="true" class="absolute top-3 right-4 flex items-center gap-1.5 print:hidden"><div class="z-10 select-none" data-state="closed"><button class="size-6.5 flex items-center justify-center rounded-md group/copy-button in-data-floating-buttons:group-[:not(:has([data-fade-overlay]))]:bg-gray-100 dark:in-data-floating-buttons:group-[:not(:has([data-fade-overlay]))]:bg-gray-800" data-testid="copy-code-button" aria-label="Copy the contents from the code block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" class="size-4 shrink-0 text-gray-400 group-hover/copy-button:text-gray-500 dark:text-white/40 dark:group-hover/copy-button:text-white/60"><path d="M14.25 5.25H7.25C6.14543 5.25 5.25 6.14543 5.25 7.25V14.25C5.25 15.3546 6.14543 16.25 7.25 16.25H14.25C15.3546 16.25 16.25 15.3546 16.25 14.25V7.25C16.25 6.14543 15.3546 5.25 14.25 5.25Z" stroke="currentColor" width="1.5" linecap="round" linejoin="round"></path><path d="M2.80103 11.998L1.77203 5.07397C1.61003 3.98097 2.36403 2.96397 3.45603 2.80197L10.38 1.77297C11.313 1.63397 12.19 2.16297 12.528 3.00097" stroke="currentColor" width="1.5" linecap="round" linejoin="round"></path></svg></button><span role="status" class="sr-only"></span></div></div><div role="presentation" style="position:relative;--scroll-area-corner-height:0px;--scroll-area-corner-width:0px;font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E" data-component-part="code-block-root" class="w-0 min-w-full max-w-full h-full dark:bg-codeblock text-sm leading-6 transition-[height] duration-300 ease-in-out code-block-background **:ring-0 **:outline-0 **:focus:ring-0 **:focus:outline-0 rounded-2xl bg-white"><div role="presentation" data-id="base-ui-_R_6dlcrrav5tccsmisnpfiulb_-viewport" tabindex="-1" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] py-3.5 px-4 overflow-y-hidden! base-ui-disable-scrollbar" style="overflow:scroll" data-component-part="scroll-area-viewport"><div role="presentation" style="min-width:fit-content" data-component-part="scroll-area-content" class="min-w-full! h-full children:my-0! children:shadow-none! children:bg-transparent!"><div class="font-mono whitespace-pre leading-6"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E;color:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4" language="text"><code language="text" numberOfLines="2"><span class="line"><span>100 YES tokens + 100 NO tokens → 100 pUSD</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">Before merging, ensure you have:</span>
<ol>
<li>Equal amounts of YES and NO tokens.</li>
<li>Approved the collateral adapter for the market type to transfer the wallet’s
outcome tokens.</li>
</ol>

Transactions</a> for nonce
creation, wallet-batch signing, and confirmation. Wait for
<code>STATE_CONFIRMED</code> before using the updated balances.</span></div></div></div></div></div><div id="panel-solidity-3-3" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="solidity-3" tabindex="0" class="prose dark:prose-invert overflow-x-auto [&amp;_[data-table-wrapper]]:![--page-padding:0px] [&amp;_[role=&quot;listitem&quot;]]:pl-4 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)_img]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child[data-table-wrapper]]:pt-0! hidden" data-component-part="tab-content"><span data-as="p">Merging outcome tokens through a collateral adapter follows this flow:</span><ul>
<li>Approve the collateral adapter to transfer the caller’s outcome tokens.</li>
<li>Call the adapter with the market’s condition ID and the amount to merge.</li>
<li>The adapter burns equal YES and NO balances and returns pUSD atomically.</li>
</ul><div role="list" class="steps ml-3.5 mt-10 mb-6"><div role="listitem" class="step group/step step-container relative flex items-start pb-5"><div data-component-part="step-line" class="absolute w-px h-[calc(100%-2.75rem)] top-11 bg-gray-200/70 dark:bg-white/10" contentEditable="false"></div><div class="absolute ml-[-13px] py-2" data-component-part="step-number" contentEditable="false"><div class="group/step-indicator relative size-7 shrink-0 rounded-full bg-gray-50 dark:bg-white/10 text-xs text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-50 font-semibold flex items-center justify-center"><div class="group-has-[a:focus-visible]/step-indicator:opacity-0">1</div></div></div><div class="w-full overflow-hidden pl-8 pr-px"><p class="mt-2 font-semibold prose dark:prose-invert text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200" contentEditable="false" data-component-part="step-title">Approve Outcome Tokens</p><div data-component-part="step-content" class="prose dark:prose-invert"><span data-as="p">First, call <code>setApprovalForAll()</code> on the Conditional Tokens contract.

<code>NegRiskCtfCollateralAdapter</code> for a negative-risk market:</span><div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 The call returns the
same amount of pUSD to the caller.</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="redeem-resolved-positions"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#redeem-resolved-positions" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="size-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-xs text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" class="size-3 shrink-0"><path d="M8.50001 6.827C8.14801 6.995 7.81801 7.225 7.52701 7.517L7.51701 7.527C6.13601 8.908 6.13601 11.146 7.51701 12.527L9.69201 14.702C11.073 16.083 13.311 16.083 14.692 14.702L14.702 14.692C16.083 13.311 16.083 11.073 14.702 9.692L13.771 8.761" stroke="currentColor" width="1.5" linecap="round" linejoin="round"></path><path d="M9.50002 11.173C9.85202 11.005 10.182 10.775 10.473 10.483L10.483 10.473C11.864 9.092 11.864 6.854 10.483 5.473L8.30802 3.298C6.92702 1.917 4.68902 1.917 3.30802 3.298L3.29802 3.308C1.91702 4.689 1.91702 6.927 3.29802 8.308L4.22902 9.239" stroke="currentColor" width="1.5" linecap="round" linejoin="round"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Redeem Resolved Positions</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Redeeming converts outcome tokens into pUSD after a market resolves. Each
winning token returns 1 pUSD, while losing tokens return 0.</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 dark:twoslash-dark bg-transparent dark:bg-transparent" numberOfLines="4" language="text"><div data-floating-buttons="true" class="absolute top-3 right-4 flex items-center gap-1.5 print:hidden"><div aria-label="Copy the contents from the code block"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" dark:group-hover/copy-button:text-white/60"><path d="M14.25 5.25H7.25C6.14543 5.25 5.25 6.14543 5.25 7.25V14.25C5.25 15.3546 6.14543 16.25 7.25 16.25H14.25C15.3546 16.25 16.25 15.3546 16.25 class="sr-only"></span></div></div><div role="presentation" style="position:relative;--scroll-area-corner-height:0px;--scroll-area-corner-width:0px;font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E" <span class="line"><span>100 YES tokens → 100 pUSD</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>100 NO tokens  → 0 pUSD</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<div role="note" aria-label="Note" class="callout my-4 px-5 py-4 overflow-hidden rounded-2xl flex gap-3 border border-blue-200 bg-blue-50 dark:border-blue-900 dark:bg-blue-600/20" data-callout-type="note"><div class="mt-0.5 w-4" data-component-part="callout-icon"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true" class="size-4 text-blue-800 dark:text-blue-300"><path d="M 9 1.6714 C 13.0371 1.6714 16.3286 4.9629 16.3286 9 C 16.3286 13.0371 13.0371 16.3286 9 16.3286 C 7.0574 16.3252 5.1953 15.552 3.8217 14.1783 C 2.448 12.8047 1.6748 10.9426 1.6714 9 C 1.6714 4.9629 4.9629 1.6714 9 1.6714 Z M 9 0 C 4.0371 0 0 4.0371 0 9 C 0 13.9629 4.0371 18 9 18 C 13.9629 18 18 13.9629 18 9 C 18 4.0371 13.9629 0 9 0 Z M 10.2857 3.8571 H 7.7143 V 10.2857 H 10.2857 V 3.8571 Z M 10.2857 11.5714 H 7.7143 V 14.1429 H 10.2857 V 11.5714 Z" fill="currentColor" stroke="none" fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div><div class="text-sm prose dark:prose-invert min-w-0 w-full [&amp;_kbd]:bg-background-light dark:[&amp;_kbd]:bg-background-dark [&amp;_code]:text-current! [&amp;_kbd]:text-current! [&amp;_a]:text-current! [&amp;_a]:border-current [&amp;_strong]:text-current! text-blue-800 dark:text-blue-300" data-component-part="callout-content"><span data-as="p">There is no redemption deadline. Winning tokens remain redeemable at any time
after resolution.</span></div></div>
<span data-as="p">Before redeeming, ensure you have:</span>
<ol>
<li>A resolved market.</li>
<li>Outcome tokens for the market.</li>
<li>Approved the collateral adapter for the market type to transfer the wallet’s
outcome tokens.</li>
</ol>

both outcomes. <code>wait()</code> returns a <code>TransactionOutcome</code> after the transaction

</code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div><span data-as="p">Redemption has no amount parameter: it redeems the wallet’s balances for
both outcomes. <code>wait()</code> returns a <code>TransactionOutcome</code> after the transaction
settles.</span></div><div id="panel-api-4-2" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="api-4" tabindex="0" class="prose dark:prose-invert overflow-x-auto [&amp;_[data-table-wrapper]]:![--page-padding:0px] [&amp;_[role=&quot;listitem&quot;]]:pl-4 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)_img]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child[data-table-wrapper]]:pt-0! hidden" data-component-part="tab-content"><span data-as="p">Build the <code>redeemPositions</code> call for a resolved market, then execute it as a
gasless wallet transaction.</span><div role="list" class="steps ml-3.5 mt-10 mb-6"><div role="listitem" class="step group/step step-container relative flex items-start pb-5"><div data-component-part="step-line" class="absolute w-px h-[calc(100%-2.75rem)] top-11 bg-gray-200/70 dark:bg-white/10" contentEditable="false"></div><div class="absolute ml-[-13px] py-2" data-component-part="step-number" contentEditable="false"><div class="group/step-indicator relative size-7 shrink-0 rounded-full bg-gray-50 dark:bg-white/10 text-xs text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-50 font-semibold flex items-center justify-center"><div class="group-has-[a:focus-visible]/step-indicator:opacity-0">1</div></div></div><div class="w-full overflow-hidden pl-8 pr-px"><p class="mt-2 font-semibold prose dark:prose-invert text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200" contentEditable="false" data-component-part="step-title">Build the Redemption Call</p><div data-component-part="step-content" class="prose dark:prose-invert"><span data-as="p">Use <code>CtfCollateralAdapter</code> at

<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    &quot;metadata&quot;: &quot;Redeem positions&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    &quot;depositWalletParams&quot;: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">      &quot;depositWallet&quot;: &quot;&lt;deposit_wallet_address&gt;&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">      &quot;deadline&quot;: &quot;&lt;unix_seconds&gt;&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">      &quot;calls&quot;: [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">          &quot;target&quot;: &quot;&lt;collateral_adapter_address&gt;&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">          &quot;value&quot;: &quot;0&quot;,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">          &quot;data&quot;: &quot;&lt;encoded_redeem_positions_calldata&gt;&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">      ]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">  }&#x27;</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div><span data-as="p">See <a class="link" href="/trading/wallets-auth#execute-gasless-transactions">Execute Gasless
Transactions</a> for nonce
creation, wallet-batch signing, and confirmation. Wait for
<code>STATE_CONFIRMED</code> before using the payout.</span></div></div></div></div></div><div id="panel-solidity-4-3" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="solidity-4" tabindex="0" class="prose dark:prose-invert overflow-x-auto [&amp;_[data-table-wrapper]]:![--page-padding:0px] [&amp;_[role=&quot;listitem&quot;]]:pl-4 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child:not(p)_img]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;:first-child[data-table-wrapper]]:pt-0! hidden" data-component-part="tab-content"><span data-as="p">Redeeming outcome tokens through a collateral adapter follows this flow:</span><ul>
<li>Approve the collateral adapter to transfer the caller’s outcome tokens.</li>
<li>After resolution, call the adapter with the market’s condition ID.</li>
<li>The adapter burns both outcome balances and returns the winning payout in
pUSD atomically.</li>
</ul><div role="list" class="steps ml-3.5 mt-10 mb-6"><div role="listitem" class="step group/step step-container relative flex items-start pb-5"><div data-component-part="step-line" class="absolute w-px h-[calc(100%-2.75rem)] top-11 bg-gray-200/70 dark:bg-white/10" contentEditable="false"></div><div class="absolute ml-[-13px] py-2" data-component-part="step-number" contentEditable="false"><div class="group/step-indicator relative size-7 shrink-0 rounded-full bg-gray-50 dark:bg-white/10 text-xs text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-50 font-semibold flex items-center justify-center"><div class="group-has-[a:focus-visible]/step-indicator:opacity-0">1</div></div></div><div class="w-full overflow-hidden pl-8 pr-px"><p class="mt-2 font-semibold prose dark:prose-invert text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-200" contentEditable="false" data-component-part="step-title">Approve Outcome Tokens</p><div data-component-part="step-content" class="prose dark:prose-invert"><span data-as="p">First, call <code>setApprovalForAll()</code> on the Conditional Tokens contract.
Approve <code>CtfCollateralAdapter</code> for a standard market or
<code>NegRiskCtfCollateralAdapter</code> for a negative-risk market:</span><div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 dark:twoslash-dark bg-transparent dark:bg-transparent" numberOfLines="1" language="solidity"><div </code></pre></div></div></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div><div role="presentation" style="position:relative;--scroll-area-corner-height:0px;--scroll-area-corner-width:0px" data-component-part="scroll-area" data-table-wrapper="true" class="min-w-0 [--page-padding:20px] flex w-[calc(100%+(var(--page-padding)*2))] my-[1em] py-[1em] -mx-(--page-padding) max-w-none [contain:inline-size]"><div role="region" data-id="base-ui-_R_tninlcrrav5tccsmisnpfiulb_-viewport" tabindex="-1" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] overflow-y-hidden! Orders you place after the\\nfire are not affected by the expired deadline — re-arm to extend\\nprotection.\\n\\nEach account may trigger auto-cancel at most 10 times per UTC day.
